[Intangible Textual Heritage](../../index)  [Buddhism](../index) 
[Zen](index)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

<div class="Section1">

<span style="font-size:20.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**The Gateless
Gate**</span><span
style="font-size:20.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">*The Gateless
Gate*</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> or
*The Gateless Barrier*</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> (Chin. Wu-wen kuan;
Jap. Mumonkan)</span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The author is
Chinese Ch'an master *Wu-men Hui-hai*</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> (</span><span
style="font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black">無門慧開</span><span style="font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> *Mumon Ekai*</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, <span
style="color:black">1183-1260).</span></span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**English
Translation**</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">By late Zen master
*Katsuki Sekida*</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> (*Two Zen
Classics*</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
26-137)</span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Original Chinese
Text**</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The original
Chinese text is taken from the following Japanese web site:</span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                 
</span>https://homepage1.nifty.com/poem-club/mumonnkan/mumonkanwoyomu.htm</span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The Chinese and
Japanese texts in this web site are taken from the book titled
*Mumonkan*</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">,
published in Japan by *Iwanami Bunkõ*</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">.</span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Chinese
Characters**</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Unfortunately a
few Chinese characters were not given in this site. Luckily these
characters are less than 1% of the text. Where there was a definition
about these ideograms, they are entered them using Chinese system (Big
5). There are also ideograms that appear as mere black boxes, without
any explanations. These are replaced with dummy characters (empty square
boxes).</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**The
Gateless Gate**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門<span
style="color:black">關</span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Wu-wen
kuan (Mumonkan)</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's
Preface**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">佛語心爲宗、無門爲法門。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Buddhism makes mind its
foundation and no-gate its gate.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">既是無門、且作麼生透。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Now, how do you pass through
this no-gate?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">豈不見道、從門入者不是家珍、從縁得者始終成壞。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">It is said that things coming
in through the gate can never be your own treasures. What is gained from
external circumstances will perish in the end.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">恁麼説話、大似無風起浪好肉抉瘡。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">However, such a saying is
already raising waves when there is no wind. It is cutting unblemished
skin.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">何況滯言句覓解會。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">掉棒打月、隔靴爬痒、有甚交渉。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">As for those who try to
understand through other people's words, they are striking at the moon
with a stick; scratching a shoe, whereas it is the foot that itches.
What concern have they with the truth?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">慧開、紹定戊子夏、首衆于東嘉龍翔。因納子請益、遂將古人公案作敲門瓦子、隨機引導學者。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">In the summer of the first year
of Jõtei, Ekai was in Ryûshõ Temple and as head monk worked with the
monks, using the cases of the ancient masters as brickbats to batter the
gate and lead them on according to their respective capacities.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">竟爾抄録、不覺成集。初不以前後敍列、共成四十八則。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The text was written down not
according to any scheme, but just to make a collection of forty-eight
cases.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">通曰無門關。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">It is called
*Mumonkan*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">, "The
Gateless Gate."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">若是箇漢、不顧危亡單刀直入。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A man of determination will
unflinchingly push his way straight forward, regardless of all
dangers.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">八臂那咤、擱他不在。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Then even the eight-armed Nata
cannot hinder him.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">縦使西天四七、東土二三、只得望風乞命。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Even the four sevens of the
West and the two threes of the East would beg for their lives.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">設或躊躇、也似隔窓看馬騎、貶得眼來、早已蹉過。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If one has no determination,
then it will be like catching a glimpse of a horse galloping past the
window: in the twinkling of an eye it will be gone.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">大道無門</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>The Great Way is gateless,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">千差有路</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Approached in a thousand ways.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">透得此關</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Once past this checkpoint</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">乾坤獨歩</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>You stride through the universe.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
1**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Jõshû's "Mu"<span style="mso-tab-count:2">                       
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">一　趙州狗子</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">趙州和尚、因僧問、狗子還有佛性也無。州云、無。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A monk asked Jõshû, "Has a dog
the Buddha Nature?" Jõshû answered, "Mu."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、參禪須透祖師關、妙悟要窮心路絶。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">In order to master Zen, you
must pass the barrier of the patriarchs. To attain this subtle
realization, you must completely cut off the way of thinking.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">祖關不透心路不絶、盡是依草附木精靈。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you do not pass the barrier,
and do not cut off the way of thinking, then you will be like a ghost
clinging to the bushes and weeds.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">且道、如何是祖師關。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Now, I want to ask you, what is
the barrier of the patriarchs?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">只者一箇無字、乃宗門一關也。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Why, it is this single word
"Mu." That is the front gate to Zen.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">遂目之曰禪宗無門關。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Therefore it is called the
"Mumonkan of Zen."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">透得過者、非但親見趙州、便可與歴代祖師把手共行、眉毛厮結同一眼見、同一耳聞。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you pass through it, you
will not only see Jõshû face to face, but you will also go hand in hand
with the successive patriarchs, entangling your eyebrows with theirs,
seeing with the same eyes, hearing with the same ears.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">豈不慶快。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Isn't that a delightful
prospect?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">莫有要透關底麼。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Wouldn't you like to pass this
barrier?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">將三百六十骨節、八萬四千毫竅、通身起箇疑團參箇無字。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Arouse your entire body with
its three hundred and sixty bones and joints and its eighty-four
thousand pores of the skin; summon up a spirit of great doubt and
concentrate on this word "Mu."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">晝夜提撕、莫作虚無會、莫作有無會。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Carry it continuously day and
night. Do not form a nihilistic conception of vacancy, or a relative
conception of "has" or "has not."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">如呑了箇熱鐵丸相似、吐又吐不出。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">It will be just as if you
swallow a red-hot iron ball, which you cannot spit out even if you
try.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">蕩盡從　前惡知惡覚、久久純熟自然内外打成—片、如唖子得夢、只許自知。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">All the illusory ideas and
delusive thoughts accumulated up to the present will be exterminated,
and when the time comes, internal and external will be spontaneously
united. You will know this, but for yourself only, like a dumb man who
has had a dream.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">驀然打發、驚天　動地。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Then all of a sudden an
explosive conversion will occur, and you will astonish the heavens and
shake the earth.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">如奪得關將軍大刀入手、逢佛殺佛、逢祖殺祖、於生死岸頭得大自在、向六道四生中遊戲三昧。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">It will be as if you snatch
away the great sword of the valiant general Kan'u and hold it in your
hand. When you meet the Buddha, you kill him; when you meet the
patriarchs, you kill them. On the brink of life and death, you command
perfect freedom; among the sixfold worlds and four modes of existence,
you enjoy a merry and playful samadhi.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">且作麼生提撕。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Now, I want to ask you again,
"How will you carry it out?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">盡平生氣力擧箇無字。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Employ every ounce of your
energy to work on this "Mu."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">若不間斷、好似法燭一點便著。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you hold on without
interruption, behold: a single spark, and the holy candle is lit!</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse** </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">狗子佛性</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>The dog, the Buddha Nature,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">全提正令</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>The pronouncement, perfect and final.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">纔渉有無</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Before you say it has or has not,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">喪身失命</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>You are a dead man on the spot.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
2**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Hyakujõ's Fox<span style="mso-tab-count:2">                    
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">二　百丈野狐</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">百丈和尚、凡參次、有一老人常隨衆聽法。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When Hyakujõ Oshõ delivered a
certain series of sermons, an old man always followed the monks to the
main hall and listened to him.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">衆人退、老人亦退。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When the monks left the hall,
the old man would also leave.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">忽一日不退。師遂問、面前立者復是何人。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">One day, however, he remained
behind, and Hyakujõ asked him, "Who are you, standing here before
me?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">老人云、諾。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The old man replied.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">某甲非人也。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"I am not a human being.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">於過去迦葉佛時曾住此山。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">In the old days of Kashyapa
Buddha, I was a head monk, living here on this mountain.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">因學人問、大修行底人還落因果也無。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">One day a student asked me,
'Does a man of enlightenment fall under the yoke of causation or
not?'</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">某甲對云、不落因果。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">I answered, 'No, he does
not.'</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">五百生墮野狐身。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Since then I have been doomed
to undergo five hundred rebirths as a fox.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">今請、和尚代一轉語貴脱野狐。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">I beg you now to give the
turning word to release me from my life as a fox.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">遂問、大修行底人、還落因果也無。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tell me, does a man of
enlightenment fall under the yoke of causation or not?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">師云、不昧因果。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Hyakujõ answered, "He does not
ignore causation."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">老人於言下大悟。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">No sooner had the old man heard
these words than he was enlightened.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">作禮云、某甲、已脱野狐身住在山後。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Making his bows, he said, "I am
emancipated from my life as a fox. I shall remain on this
mountain.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">敢告和尚。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">乞、依亡僧事例。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">I have a favor to ask of you:
would you please bury my body as that of a dead monk."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">師、令維那白槌告衆、食後送亡僧。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Hyakujõ had the director of the
monks strike with the gavel and inform everyone that after the midday
meal there would be a funeral service for a dead monk.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">大衆言議、一衆皆安、涅槃堂又無人病。何故如是。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The monks wondered at this,
saying, "Everyone is in good health; nobody is in the sick ward. What
does this mean?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">食後只見師領衆至山後嵒下、以杖挑出一死野狐、乃依火葬。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">After the meal Hyakujõ led the
monks to the foot of a rock on the far side of the mountain and with his
staff poked out the dead body of a fox and performed the ceremony of
cremation.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">師、至晩上堂、擧前因縁。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">That evening he ascended the
rostrum and told the monks the whole story.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">黄蘗便問、古人錯祗對一轉語、墮五百生野狐身、轉轉不錯合作箇甚麼。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Õbaku thereupon asked him, "The
old man gave the wrong answer and was doomed to be a fox for five
hundred rebirths. Now, suppose he had given the right answer, what would
have happened then?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">師云、近前來與伊道。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Hyakujõ said, "You come here to
me, and I will tell you."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">黄蘗遂近前、與師一掌。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Õbaku went up to Hyakujõ and
boxed his ears.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">師拍手笑云、將謂、胡鬚赤。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">更有赤鬚胡。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Hyakujõ clapped his hands with
a laugh and exclaimed, "I was thinking that the barbarian had a red
beard, but now I see before me the red-bearded barbarian
himself."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、不落因果、爲甚墮野狐。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Not falling under causation:
how could this make the monk a fox?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">不昧因果、爲甚脱野狐。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Not ignoring causation: how
could this make the old man emancipated?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">若向者裏著得一隻眼、便知得前百丈贏得風流五百生。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you come to understand this,
you will realize how old Hyakujõ would have enjoyed five hundred
rebirths as a fox.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse** </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">不落不昧</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Not falling, not ignoring:</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">兩采一賽</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Two faces of one die.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">不昧不落</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Not ignoring, not falling:</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">千錯萬錯</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>A thousand errors, a million mistakes.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
3**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Gutei
Raises a Finger<span style="mso-tab-count:2">                   
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">三　倶胝堅指</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">倶胝和尚、凡有詰問、唯擧一指。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Whenever Gutei Oshõ was asked
about Zen, he simply raised his finger.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">後有童子。因外人問、和尚説何法要。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Once a visitor asked Gutei's
boy attendant, "What does your master teach?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">童子亦堅指頭。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The boy too raised his
finger.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">胝聞遂以刃斷其指。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Hearing of this, Gutei cut off
the boy's finger with a knife.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">童子、負痛號哭而去。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The boy, screaming with pain,
began to run away.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">胝復召之。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">童子廻首。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">胝却　堅起指。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Gutei called to him, and when
he turned around, Gutei raised his finger.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">童子忽然領悟。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The boy suddenly became
enlightened.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">胝將順世、謂衆曰、吾得天龍一指頭禪、一生受用不盡。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When Gutei was about to pass
away, he said to his assembled monks, "I obtained one-finger Zen from
Tenryû and used it all my life but still did not exhaust it."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">言訖示滅。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When he had finished saying
this, he entered into eternal Nirvana.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、倶胝並童子悟處、不在指頭上。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The enlightenment of Gutei and
of the boy does not depend on the finger.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">若向者裏見得、天龍同倶胝並童子興自己一串穿却。　</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you understand this, Tenryû,
Gutei, the boy, and you yourself are all run through with one
skewer.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse** </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">倶胝鈍置老天龍</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">    </span>Gutei made a fool of old Tenryû,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">利刃單提勘小童</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">    </span>Emancipating the boy with a single slice,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">巨靈擡手無多子</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">    </span>Just as Kyorei cleaved Mount Kasan</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">分破華山千万重</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">    </span>To let the Yellow River run through.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
4**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> The
Western Barbarian with No Beard<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                          </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">四　胡子無髭</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">或庵曰、西天胡子、因甚無髭。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Wakuan said, "Why has the
Western Barbarian no beard?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、參須實參、悟須實悟。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Study should be real study,
enlightenment should be real enlightenment.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">者箇胡子、直須親見一回始得。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">You should once meet this
barbarian directly to be really intimate with him.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">説親見、早成兩箇。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">But saying you are really
intimate with him already divides you into two.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse** </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">癡人面前</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Don't discuss your dream</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">不可説夢</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Before a fool.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">胡子髭無</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Barbarian with no beard</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">惺惺添<span lang="JA"
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span></span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span>Obscures the clarity.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
5**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Kyõgen's "Man up in a Tree"<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                   </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">五　香嚴上樹</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">香嚴和尚云、如人上樹、口啣樹枝、手不攀枝、脚不踏樹。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Kyõgen Oshõ said, "It is like a
man up in a tree hanging from a branch with his mouth; his hands grasp
no bough, his feet rest on no limb.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">樹下有人問西來意、不對即違他所問、若對又喪身失命。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Someone appears under the tree
and asks him, 'What is the meaning of Bodhidharma's coming from the
West?' If he does not answer, he fails to respond to the question. If he
does answer, he will lose his life.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">正恁麼時、作麼生對。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">What would you do in such a
situation?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、縱有懸河之辨、惣用不著。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Even if your eloquence flows
like a river, it is of no avail.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">説得一大藏教、亦用不著。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Though you can expound the
whole of Buddhist literature, it is of no use.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若向者裏對得著、活却從前死路頭、死却從前活路頭。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you solve this problem, you
will give life to the way that has been dead until this moment and
destroy the way that has been alive up to now.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">其或未然、直待當來問彌勒。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Otherwise you must wait for
Maitreya Buddha and ask him.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">香嚴眞杜撰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Kyõgen is truly
thoughtless;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">惡毒無盡限</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">His vice and poison are
endless.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">唖却納僧口</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">He stops up the mouths of the
monks,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">通身迸鬼眼</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">And devil's eyes sprout from
their bodies.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
6**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> The
Buddha Holds Out a Flower<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                        </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">六　世尊拈花</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">世尊、昔、在靈山會上拈花示衆。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When Shakyamuni Buddha was at
Mount Grdhrakuta, he held out a flower to his listeners.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">是時、衆皆默然。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Everyone was silent.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">惟迦葉者破顔微笑。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Only Mahakashyapa broke into a
broad smile.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">世尊云、吾有正方眼藏、涅槃妙心、實相無相、微妙法門、不立文字、教外別傳、付囑摩訶迦葉。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The Buddha said, "I have the
True Dharma Eye, the Marvelous Mind of Nirvana, the True Form of the
Formless, and the Subtle Dharma Gate, independent of words and
transmitted beyond doctrine. This I have entrusted to
Mahakashyapa."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、黄面瞿曇、傍若無人。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Golden-faced Gautama really
disregarded his listeners.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">壓良爲賤、縣羊頭賣狗肉。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">He made the good look bad and
sold dog's meat labeled as mutton.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">將謂、多少奇特。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">He himself thought it was
wonderful.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">只如當時大衆都笑、正方眼藏、作麼生傳。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If, however, everyone in the
audience had laughed, how could he have transmitted his True Eye?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">設使迦葉不笑、正方眼藏又作麼生傳。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">And again, if Mahakashyapa had
not smiled, how could the Buddha have transmitted it?<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若道正方眼藏有傳授、黄面老子、誑</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black">閭閻。</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you say the True Dharma Eye
can be transmitted, then the golden-faced old man would be a city
slicker who cheats the country bumpkin.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若道無傳授、爲甚麼獨許迦葉。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you say it cannot be
transmitted, then why did the Buddha approve of Mahakashyapa?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">拈起花來</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Holding
out a flower,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">尾巴已露</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The
Buddha betrayed his curly tail.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">迦葉破顔</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Heaven
and earth were bewildered,<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">人天罔措</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">At
Mahakashyapa's smile.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
7**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Jõshû's "Wash Your Bowl"<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">七　趙州洗鉢</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">趙州、因僧問、其甲乍入叢林。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A monk said to Jõshû, "I have
just entered this monastery.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">乞師指示。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Please teach me."<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">州云、喫粥了也未。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Have you eaten your rice
porridge?" asked Jõshû.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">僧云、喫粥了也。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Yes, I have," replied the
monk.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">州云、洗鉢盂去。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Then you had better wash your
bowl," said Jõshû.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">其僧有省。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">With this the monk gained
insight.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、趙州開口見膽、露出心肝。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When he opens his mouth, Jõshû
shows his gallbladder. He displays his heart and liver.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">者僧聽事不眞、喚鐘作甕。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">I wonder if this monk really
did hear the truth. I hope he did not mistake the bell for a jar.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">只爲分明極</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Endeavoring to interpret
clearly,<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">翻令所得遲</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">You retard your
attainment.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">早知燈是火</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Don't you know that flame is
fire?<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">飯熟已多時</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Your rice has long been
cooked.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
8**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Keichû
the Wheelmaker<span style="mso-tab-count:2">              
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">八　奚仲造車</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">月庵和尚問僧、奚仲造車一百輻。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Gettan Oshõ said, "Keichû, the
first wheelmaker, made a cart whose wheels had a hundred spokes.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">拈却兩頭、去却輻、明甚麼邊事。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Now, suppose you took a cart
and removed both the wheels and the axle. What would you have?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、若也直下明得、眼、似流星、機、如掣電。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If anyone can directly master
this topic, his eye will be like a shooting star, his spirit like a
flash of lightning.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">機輪轉處</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When
the spiritual wheels turn,<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">達者猶迷</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Even
the master fails to follow them.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">四維上下</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">They
travel in all directions, above and below,<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">南北東西</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">North,
south, east, and west.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
9**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Daitsû
Chishõ Buddha<span style="mso-tab-count:2">                 
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">九　大通智勝</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">興陽讓和尚、因僧問、大通智勝佛、十劫坐道場、佛法不現前、不得成佛道時如何。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A monk asked Kõyõ Seijõ,
"Daitsû Chishõ Buddha sat in zazen for ten *kalpas*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> and
could not attain Buddhahood. He did not become a Buddha. How could this
be?"<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">讓曰、其問甚諦當。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Seijõ said, "Your question is
quite self-explanatory."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">僧云、既是坐道場、爲甚麼不得成佛道。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The monk asked, "He meditated
so long; why could he not attain Buddhahood?"<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">讓曰、爲伊不成佛。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Seijõ said, "Because he did not
become a Buddha."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、只許老胡知、不許老胡會。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">I allow the barbarian's
realization, but I do not allow his understanding.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">凡夫若知、既是聖人。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When an ignorant man realizes
it, he is a sage.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">聖人若會、既是凡夫。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When a sage understands it, he
is ignorant.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">了身何似了心休</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Better
emancipate your mind than your body;<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">了得心</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black">身不愁</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When
the mind is emancipated, the body is free,<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若也身心倶了了</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When
both body and mind are emancipated,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">神仙何必更封候</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Even
gods and spirits ignore worldly power.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
10**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Seizei
Is Utterly Destitude<span style="mso-tab-count:2">                    
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">十　清税弧貧</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">曹山和尚、因僧問云、清税弧貧。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Seizei said to Sõzan, "Seizei
is utterly destitude.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">乞、師賑濟。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Will you give him
support?"<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山云、税闍梨。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Sõzan called out,
"Seizei!"<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">税、應諾。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Seizei responded, "Yes,
sir!"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山曰、青原白家酒、三盞喫了、猶道未沾唇。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Sõzan said, "You have finished
three cups of the finest wine in China, and still you say you have not
yet moistened your lips!"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、清税輸機、是何心行。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Seizei pretended to retreat.
What was his scheme?<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">曹山具眼、深辨來機。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Sõzan had the eye of Buddha and
saw through his opponent's motive.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">然雖如是、且道、那裏是税闍梨、喫酒處。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">However, I want to ask you, at
what point did Seizei drink wine?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">貧似范丹</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Poverty
like Hantan's,<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">氣如項羽</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Mind
like Kõu's;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">活計雖無</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">With no
means of livelihood,<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">敢與鬪富</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">He
dares to rival the richest.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
11**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Jõshû
Sees the Hermits<span style="mso-tab-count:2">             
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">十一　州勘庵主</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">趙州、到一庵主處問、有麼有麼。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Jõshû went to a hermit's
cottage and asked, "Is the master in? Is the master in?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">主、堅起拳頭。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The hermit raised his
fist.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">州云、水淺不是泊</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">舡</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">處。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">便行。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Jõshû said, "The water is too
shallow to anchor here," and he went away.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">又到一庵主處云、有麼有麼。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Coming to another hermit's
cottage, he asked again, "Is the master in? Is the master in?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">主亦堅起拳頭。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">This hermit, too, raised his
fist.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">州云、能縱能奪、能殺能活。便作禮。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Jõshû said, "Free to give, free
to take, free to kill, free to save," and he made a deep bow.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、一般堅起拳頭、爲甚麼肯一箇、不肯一箇。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Both raised their fists; why
was the one accepted and the other rejected?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">且道、</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black">訛在甚處。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tell me, what is the difficulty
here?<span style="color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若向者裏下得一轉語、便見趙州舌頭無骨、扶起放倒、得大自在。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you can give a turning word
to clarify this problem, you will realize that Jõshû's tongue has no
bone in it, now helping others up, now knocking them down, with perfect
freedom.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">雖然如是爭奈、趙州却被二庵主勘破。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">However, I must remind you: the
two hermits could also see through Jõshû.<span
style="color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若道二庵主有優劣、未具參學眼。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you say there is anything to
choose between the two hermits, you have no eye of realization.<span
style="color:black;
mso-fareast-language:JA"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若道無優劣、亦未具參　學眼。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you say there is no choice
between the two, you have no eye of realization.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">眼流星</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">           </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The eye
like a shooting star,<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">機掣電</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">           </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The
spirit like a lighting;<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">殺人刀</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">           </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A
death-dealing blade,<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">活人劍</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">           </span></span><span
