style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A
life-giving sword.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
12**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Zuigan
Calls His Master<span style="mso-tab-count:2">                        
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">十二　巖喚主人</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">瑞巖彦和尚、毎日自喚主人公、復自應諾。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Zuigan Gen Oshõ called to
himself every day, "Master!" and answered, "Yes, sir!"<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">乃云、惺惺着。</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black">。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Then he would say, "Be wide
awake!" and answer, "Yes, sir!"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">他時異日、莫受人瞞。</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">□□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black">。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Henceforward, never be
deceived by others!" "No, I won't!"<span
style="color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、瑞巖老子、自買自賣、弄出許多神頭鬼面。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Old Zuigan buys and sells
himself. He takes out a lot of god-masks and devil-masks and puts them
on and plays with them.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">何故。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">What for, eh?</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">。一箇喚底、一箇應底。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">一箇惺惺底、一箇不受人瞞底。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">One calling and the other
answering; one wide awake, the other saying he will never be
deceived.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">認着依前還不是。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you stick to any of them,
you will be a failure.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若也傚他、惣是野狐見解。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you imitate Zuigan, you will
play the fox.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">學道之人不識眞</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Clinging
to the deluded way of consciousness,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">只爲從前認識神</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Students
of the Way do not realize truth.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無量劫來生死本</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The
seed of birth and death through endless eons:<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">癡人喚作本來人</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The
fool calls it the true original self.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
13**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Tokusan Holds His Bowls<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                     </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">十三　徳山托鉢</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">徳山、一日托鉢下堂。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">One day Tokusan went down
toward the dining room, holding his bowls.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">見雪峰問者老漢鐘未鳴鼓未響、托鉢向甚處去、山便回方丈。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Seppõ met him and asked, "Where
are you off to with your bowls? The bell has not rung, and the drum has
not sounded." Tokusan turned and went back to his room.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">峰擧似巖頭。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頭云、大小徳山未會末後句。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Seppõ mentioned this to Gantõ,
who remarked, "Tokusan is renowned, but he does not know the last
word."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山聞令侍者喚巖頭來、問曰、汝不肯老僧那。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tokusan heard about this remark
and sent his attendant to fetch Gantõ. "You do not approve of me?" he
asked.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">巖頭密啓其意。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Gantõ whispered his
meaning.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山乃休去。明日陞座、果與尋常不同。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tokusan said nothing at the
time, but the next day he ascended the rostrum, and behold! he was very
different from usual!</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">巖頭至僧堂前、拊掌大笑云、且喜得老漢會末後句。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Gantõ, going toward the front
of the hall, clapped his hands and laughed loudly, saying,
"Congratulations! Our old man has got hold of the last word!</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">他後天下人、不奈伊何。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">From now on, nobody in this
whole country can outdo him!"<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、若是未後句、巖頭徳山倶未夢見在。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">As for the last word, neither
Gantõ nor Tokusan has ever dreamed of it!</span>

<span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">撿</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">點將來、好似一棚傀儡。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When you look into the matter,
you find they are like puppets on the shelf!</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">識得最初句</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you realize the first,<span
style="color:
black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">便會末後句</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">You master the last.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">末後與最初</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The first and the last<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">不是者一句</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Are not one word.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
14**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Nansen
Cuts the Cat in Two<span style="mso-tab-count:2">                
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">十四　南泉斬猫</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">南泉和尚因東西堂爭猫兒。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Nansen Oshõ saw monks of the
Eastern and Western halls quarreling over a cat.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">泉乃提起云、大衆道得即救、道不得即斬却也。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">He held up the cat and said,
"If you can give an answer, you will save the cat. If not, I will kill
it."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">衆無對。泉遂斬之。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">No one could answer, and Nansen
cut the cat in two.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">晩趙州外歸。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">泉擧似州。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">That evening Jõshû returned,
and Nansen told him of the incident.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">州乃脱履安頭上而出。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Jõshû took off his sandal,
placed it on his head, and walked out.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">泉云、子若在即救得猫兒。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"If you had been there, you
would have saved the cat," Nansen remarked.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、且道、趙州頂草鞋意作麼生。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tell me, what did Jõshû mean
when he put the sandal on his head?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若向者裏下得一轉語、便見南泉令不虚行。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you can give a turning word
on this, you will see that Nansen's decree was carried out with good
reason.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">其或未然險。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If not, "Danger!"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">趙州若在</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Had
Jõshû been there,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">倒行此令</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">He
would have done the opposite;<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">奪却刀子</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When
the sword is snatched away,<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">南泉乞命</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Even
Nansen begs for his life.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
15**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Tõzan's Sixty Blows<span style="mso-tab-count:2">                   
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">十五　洞山三頓</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">雲門、因洞山參次、門問曰、近離甚處。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tõzan came to study with Unmon.
Unmon asked, "Where are you from?"<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山云、査渡。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"From Sato," Tõzan
replied.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">門曰、夏在甚處。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Where were you during the
summer?"<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山云、湖南報慈。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Well, I was at the monastery
of Hõzu, south of the lake."<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">門曰、幾時離彼。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"When did you leave there,"
Unmon asked.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山云、八月二十五。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"On August 25" was Tõzan's
reply.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">門曰、放汝三頓棒。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"I spare you sixty blows,"
Unmon said.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山至明日却上問訊。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">昨日蒙和尚放三頓棒。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The next day Tõzan came to
Unmon and said, "Yesterday you said you spared me sixty blows.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">不知過在甚麼處。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">I beg to ask you, where was I
at fault?"<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">門曰、飯袋子、江西湖南便恁麼去。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Oh, you rice bag!" shouted
Unmon. "What makes you wander about, now west of the river, now south of
the lake?"<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山於此大悟。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tõzan thereupon came to a
mighty enlightenment experience.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、雲門、當時便與本分草料、使洞山別有生機一路、家門不致寂寥。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If Unmon had given Tõzan the
true food of Zen and encouraged him to develop an active Zen spirit, his
school would not have declined as it did.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">一夜在是非海裏著到、直待天明再來、又與他注破。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tõzan had an agonizing struggle
through the whole night, lost in the sea of right and wrong. He reached
a complete impasse. After waiting for the dawn, he again went to Unmon,
and Unmon again made him a picture book of Zen.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">洞山直下悟去、未是性燥。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Even though he was directly
enlightened, Tõzan could not be called brilliant.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">且問諸人、洞山三頓棒、合喫不合喫。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Now, I want to ask you, should
Tõzan have been given sixty blows or not?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若道合喫、草木叢林皆合喫棒。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you say yes, you admit that
all the universe should be beaten.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若道不合喫、雲門又成誑語。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you say no, then you accuse
Unmon of telling a lie.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">向者裏明得、方與洞山出一口氣。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you really understand the
secret, you will be able to breathe out Zen spirit with the very mouth
of Tõzan.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">獅子教兒迷子訣</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The
lion had a secret to puzzle his cub;<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">擬前跳躑早翻身</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The cub
crouched, leaped, and dashed forward.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無端再敍當頭著</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The
second time, a casual move led to checkmate.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">前箭猶輕後箭深</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The
first arrow was light, but the second went deep.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
16**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> When
the Bell Sounds<span style="mso-tab-count:2">               
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">十六　鐘聲七條</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">雲門曰、世界恁麼廣闊。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Unmon said, "The world is vast
and wide.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">因甚向鐘聲裏披七條。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Why do you put on your
seven-piece robe at the sound of the bell?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、大凡參禪學道、切忌、隨聲遂色。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">In studying Zen, you should not
be swayed by sounds and forms.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">縱使聞聲悟道、見色明心也是尋常。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Even though you attain insight
when hearing a voice or seeing a form, this is simply the ordinary way
of things.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">殊不知、納僧家、騎聲蓋色、頭頭上明、著著上妙。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Don't you know that the real
Zen student commands sounds, controls forms, is clear-sighted at every
event and free on every occasion?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">然雖如是。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">且道、聲來耳畔、耳往聲邊。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Granted you are free, just tell
me: Does the sound come to the ear or does the ear go to the
sound?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">直饒響寂雙忘、到此如何話會。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If both sound and silence die
away, at such a juncture how could you talk of Zen?<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若將耳聽應難會、眼處聞聲方始親。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">While listening with you ear,
you cannot tell. When hearing with your eye, you are truly
intimate.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">會則事同一家</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">With
realization, things make one family;<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">不會萬別千差</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Without
realization, things are separated in a thousand ways.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">不會事同一家</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Without
realization, things make one family;<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">會則萬別千差</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">With
realization, things are separated in a thousand ways.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
17**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Chû
the National Teacher Gives Three Calls<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">           </span><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">              </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">十七　國師三喚</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">國師三喚侍者。侍者三應。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The National Teacher called his
attendant three times, and three times the attendant responded.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">國師云、將謂吾辜負汝、元來却是汝辜負吾。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The National Teacher said, "I
long feared that I was betraying you, but really it was you who were
betraying me."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、國師三喚、舌頭墮地。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The National Teacher called
three times, and his tongue fell to the ground.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">侍者三應、和光吐出。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The attendant responded three
times, and he gave his answer with brilliance.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">國師年老心孤、按牛頭喫草。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The National Teacher was old
and lonely; he held the cow's head and forced it to eat grass.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">侍者未肯承當。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">
</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The attendant would have none
of it;<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">美食不中飽人</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black">、且道、那裏是他辜負處。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">delicious food has little
attraction for a man who is satiated. Tell me, at what point was the
betrayal?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">國淨才子貴、家富小兒嬌。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When the country is
flourishing, talent is prized. When the home is wealthy, the children
are proud.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">鉄枷無孔要人擔</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">He
carried and iron yoke with no hole</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">累及兒孫不等閑</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">And
left a curse to trouble his descendants.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">欲得</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black">門并</span><span lang="JA" style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">戸</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you
want to hold up the gate and the doors,<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">更須赤脚上刀山</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">You
must climb a mountain of swords with bare feet.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
18**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Tõzan's "Masagin"<span style="mso-tab-count:2">                       
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">十八　洞山三斤</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">洞山和尚、因僧問、如何是佛。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A monk asked Tõzan, "What is
Buddha?"<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山云、麻三斤。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tõzan replied, "Masagin!"
\[three pounds of flax\].</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、洞山老人、參得些蚌蛤禪、纔開兩片露出肝腸。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Old Tõzan attained the poor Zen
of a clam. He opened the two halves of the shell a little and exposed
all the liver and intestines inside.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">然雖如是、且道、向甚處見洞山。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">But tell me, how do you see
Tõzan?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">突出麻三斤</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Three pounds of flax" came
sweeping along;<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">言親意更親</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Close were the words, but
closer was the meaning.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">來説是非者</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Those who argue about right and
wrong<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">便是是非人</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Are those enslaved by right and
wrong.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
19**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Nansen's "Ordinary Mind Is the Way"<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                          </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">十九　平常是道</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">南泉、因趙州問、如何是道。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Jõshû asked Nansen, "What is
the Way?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">泉云、平常心是道。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Ordinary mind is the Way,"
Nansen replied.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">州云、還可趣向否。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Shall I try to seek after it?"
Jõshû asked.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">泉云、擬向即乖。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"If you try for it, you will
become separated from it," responded Nansen.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">州云、不擬爭知是道。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"How can I know the Way unless
I try for it?" persisted Jõshû.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">泉云、道不屬知、不屬不知。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Nansen said, "The Way is not a
matter of knowing or not knowing.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">知是妄覺、不知是無記。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Knowing is delusion; not
knowing is confusion.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若眞達不擬之道、猶如太虚廓然洞豁。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When you have really reached
the true Way beyond doubt, you will find it as vast and boundless as
outer space.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">豈可強是非也。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">How can it be talked about on
the level of right and wrong?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">州於言下頓悟。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">With these words, Jõshû came to
a sudden realization.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、南泉被趙州發問、直得瓦解氷消、分疎不下。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Nansen dissolved and melted
away before Jõshû's question, and could not offer a plausible
explanation.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">趙州縱饒悟去、更參三十年始得。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Even though Jõshû comes to a
realization, he must delve into it for another thirty years before he
can fully understand it.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">春有百花秋有月</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span>The spring flowers, the autumn
moon;</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">夏有涼風冬有雪</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span>Summer breezes, winter snow.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">若無閑事挂心頭</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span>If useless things do not clutter your
mind,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA">更是人間好時節</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span>You have the best days of your
life.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
20**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> The
Man of Great Strength<span style="mso-tab-count:2">                   
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">二十　大力量人</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">松源和尚云、大力量人、因甚擡脚不起。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Shõgen Oshõ asked, "Why is it
that a man of great strength does not lift his legs?"<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">又云、開口不在舌頭上。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">And he also said, "It is not
the tongue he speaks with."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、松源可謂、傾腸倒腹。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">It must be said that Shõgen
shows us all his stomach and intestines.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">只是欠人承當。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">But alas, no one can appreciate
him!</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">縱饒直下承當、正好來無門處喫痛棒。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">And even if someone could
appreciate him, let him come to me, and I'll beat him severely.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">何故。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Why?<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">。要識眞金、火裏看。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you want to find pure gold,
you must see it through fire.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">擡脚踏翻香水海</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Lifting
his leg, he kicks up the Scented Ocean;<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">低頭俯視四禪天</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Lowering
his head, he looks down on the fourth Dhyana heaven.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">一箇渾身無處著請</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">            </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">There
is no space vast enough for his body—<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">續一句</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                         </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Now,
somebody write the last line here.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
21**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Unmon's "Kanshiketsu"<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                          </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">二十一　雲門屎</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">橛</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-fareast-language:JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">雲門、因僧問、如何是佛。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A monk asked Unmon, "What is
Buddha?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">門云、乾屎</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">橛</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Unmon replied, "Kanshiketsu!"
\[A dry shit-stick.\]</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、雲門可謂、家貧難辨素食、事忙不及草書。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Unmon was too poor to prepare
plain food, too busy to speak from notes.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">動便將屎</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">橛</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">來、</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black">門挂戸。</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">He hurriedly took up
*shiketsu*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> to
support the Way.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">佛法興衰可見。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The decline of Buddhism was
thus foreshadowed.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">閃電光</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">           </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Lightning
flashing,<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">撃石化</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">           </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Sparks
shooting;<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">貶得眼</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">           </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A
moment's blinking,<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">巳蹉過</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">           </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Missed
forever.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
22**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Kashyapa's "Knock Down the Flagpole"<span style="mso-tab-count:1">     
</span><span style="mso-tab-count:1">              </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">二十二　迦葉刹竿</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">迦葉、因阿難問云、世尊傳金襴袈裟外、別傳何物。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Ananda asked Kashyapa, "The
World-honored One gave you the golden robe; did he give you anything
else?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">葉喚云、阿難。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Ananda!" cried
Kashyapa.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">難、應諾。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Yes, sir!" answered
Ananda.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">葉云、倒却門前刹竿著。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Knock down the flagpole at the
gate," said Kashyapa.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、若向者裏下得一轉語親切、便見靈山一會儼然未散。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you can give a turning word
at this point, you will see that the meeting at Mount Grdhrakuta is
still solemnly continuing.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">其或未然、毘婆尸佛、早留心、直至而今不得妙。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If not, then this is what
Vipasyin Buddha worried about from remote ages; up to now he has still
not acquired the essence.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">問處何如答處親</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tell me—question or
answer—which was more intimate?<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">幾人於此眼生筋</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Many have knit their brows over
this;<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">兄呼弟鷹揚家醜</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Elder brother calls, younger
brother answers, and they betray the family secret.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">不屬陰陽別是春</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">They had a special spring, not
one of yin and yang.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
23**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Think
Neither Good Nor Evil<span style="mso-tab-count:2">             
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">二十三　不思善惡</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">六祖、因明上座、趁至大</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">庾</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">嶺。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The Sixth Patriarch was pursued
by the monk Myõ as far as Taiyu Mountain.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">祖見明至、即擲衣鉢於石上云、此衣表信。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">可力爭耶、任君將去。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The patriarch, seeing Myõ
coming, laid the robe and bowl on a rock and said, "This robe represents
the faith; it should not be fought over. If you want to take it away,
take it now."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">明遂擧之如山不動、踟</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black">悚慄。</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">明白、我來　求法、非爲衣也。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Myõ tried to move it, but it
was as heavy as a mountain and would not budge. Faltering and trembling,
he cried out, "I came for the Dharma, not for the robe.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">願行者開示。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">I beg you, please give me your
instruction."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">祖云、不思善、不思惡、正與麼時、那箇是明上座本來面目。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The patriarch said, "Think
neither good nor evil. At this very moment, what is the original self of
the monk Myõ?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">明當下大悟、遍體汗流。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">At these words, Myõ was
directly illuminated. His whole body was covered with sweat.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">泣涙作禮、問曰、上來密語密意外、還更　有意旨否。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">He wept and bowed, saying,
"Besides the secret words and the secret meaning you have just now
revealed to me, is there anything else, deeper still?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">祖曰、我今爲汝説者、即非密也。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The patriarch said, "What I
have told you is no secret at all.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">汝若返照自己面目、密却在汝邊。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When you look into your own
true self, whatever is deeper is found right there."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">明云、其申雖在黄梅隨衆、實未省自己面目。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Myõ said, "I was with the monks
under Õbai for many years but I could not realize my true self.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">今蒙指授入處、如人飲水冷暖自知。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">But now, receiving your
instruction, I know it is like a man drinking water and knowing whether
it is cold or warm.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">今行者即是某甲師也。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">My lay brother, you are now my
teacher."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">祖云、汝若如是則吾與汝同師黄梅。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The patriarch said, "If you say
so, but let us both call Õbai our teacher.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">善自護持。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Be mindful to treasure and hold
fast to what you have attained."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無問曰、六祖可謂、是事出急家老婆心切。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The Sixth Patriarch was, so to
speak, hurried into helping a man in an emergency, and he displayed a
grandmotherly kindness.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">譬如新茘支剥了殻去了核、送在</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">你</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">口裏、只要</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">你</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">嚥一嚥。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">It is as though he peeled a
fresh lichi, removed the seed, put it in your mouth, and asked you to
swallow it down.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">描不成兮畫不就</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">You
cannot describe it; you cannot picture it;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">贊不及兮休生受</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">You
cannot admire it; don't try to eat it raw.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">本來面目没處藏</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Your
true self has nowhere to hide;<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">世界壞時渠不朽</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When
the world is destroyed, it is not destroyed.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
24**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Fuketsu's Speech and Silence<span style="mso-tab-count:2">              
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">二十四　離却語言</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">風穴和尚、因僧問、語默渉離微、如何通不犯。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A monk asked Fuketsu, "Both
speech and silence are faulty in being *ri*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> \[</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">離</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> inward
action of mind\] or *bi*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
\[</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black">微</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
outward action of mind\]. How can we escape these faults?"<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">穴云、長憶江南三月裏、鷓鴣啼處百花香。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Fuketsu said,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">              </span>"I always remember the
spring in Kõnan,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">              </span>Where the partridges
sing;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">              </span>How fragrant the countless
flowers!"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、風穴機如掣電得路便行。</span><span
