style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Fuketsu's Zen spirit was like
lightning and opened a clear passage.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">爭奈坐前人舌頭不斷。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">However, he was entangled in
the monk's words and could not cut them off.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若向者裏見得親切、自有出身之路。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you can really grasp the
problem, you can readily find the way out.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">且離却語言三昧、道將一句來。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Now, putting language samadhi
aside, say it in your own words.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">不露風骨句</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">He does not use a refined
phrase;<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">未語先分付</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Before speaking, he has already
handed it over.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">進歩口喃喃</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you chatter on and on,<span
style="color:
black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">知君大罔措</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">You will find you have lost
your way.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
25**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Kyõzan's Dream<span style="mso-tab-count:2">              
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">二十五　三座説法</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">仰山和尚、夢見往彌勒所、安第三座。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">In a dream Kyõzan Oshõ went to
Maitreya's place and was led in to sit in the third seat.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">有一尊者、白槌云、今日當第三座説法。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A senior monk struck with a
gavel and said, "Today the one in the third seat will speak."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山乃起白槌云、摩訶衍法離四句、絶百非。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Kyõzan rose and, striking with
the gavel, said, "The truth of Mahayana is beyond the four propositions
and transcends the hundred negations.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">諦聽、諦聽。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Taichõ! Taichõ!" \[Hear the
truth!\]</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、且道、是説法不説法、開口即失、閉口又喪。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Now tell me, did Kyõzan preach
or did he not not? If he opens his mouth, he is lost; if he seals his
mouth, he is lost.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">不開不閉、十万八千。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Even if he neither opens nor
shuts his mouth, he is a hundred and eight thousand \[miles away from
the truth\].</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">白日晴天</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">In
broad daylight, under the blue sky,<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">夢中説夢</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">He
forges a dream in a dream;<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">捏怪捏怪</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">He
makes up a monstrous story<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">誑</span><span lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black">一衆</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">And
tries to deceive the whole crowd.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
26**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Two
Monks Roll Up the Blinds<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                        </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">二十六　二僧卷簾</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">清涼大法眼、因僧齋前上參。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">眼以手指簾。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When the monks assembled before
the midday meal to listen to his lecture, the great Hõgen of Seiryõ
pointed at the bamboo blinds.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">時有二僧、同去卷簾。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Two monks simultaneously went
and rolled them up.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">眼曰、一得一失。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Hõgen said, "One gain, one
loss."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、且道、是誰得誰失。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tell me, who gained and who
lost?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若向者裏著得一隻眼、便知清涼國師敗闕處。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you have an eye to penetrate
the secret, you will see where Seiryõ Kokushi failed.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">然雖如是、切忌向得失裏商量。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">However, I warn you strongly
against discussing gain and loss.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">卷起明明徹太空</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Rolling
up the blinds, the great sky is open,<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">太空猶末合吾宗</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">But the
great sky does not come up to Zen.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">爭似從空都放下</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Why
don't you throw them all down from the sky,<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">綿綿密密不通風</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">And
keep your practice so close that no air can escape?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
27**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Nansen's "Not Mind, Not Buddha, Not Things"<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">     </span><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">              </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">二十七　不是心佛</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">南泉和尚、因僧問云、還有不與人説底法麼。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A monk asked Nansen, "Is there
any Dharma that has not been preached to the people?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">泉云、有。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Nansen answered, "There
is."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">僧云、如何是不與人説底法。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"What is the truth that has not
been taught?" asked the monk.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">泉云、不是心、不是佛、不是物。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Nansen said, "It is not mind;
it is not Buddha; it is not things."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、南泉被者一問、直得揣盡家私、郎當不少。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">At this question, Nansen used
up all his treasure and was not a little confused.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">叮嚀損君徳</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Talking too much spoils your
virtue;<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無言眞有功</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Silence is truly
unequaled.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">任從滄海變</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Let the mountains become the
sea;<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">終不爲君通</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1"> </span></span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">I'll give you no
comment.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
28**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Ryûtan
Blows Out the Candle<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                           </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">二十八　久嚮龍潭</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">龍潭、因徳山請益抵夜。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tokusan asked Ryûtan about Zen
far into the night.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">潭云、夜深。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">At last Ryûtan said, "The night
is late.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">子何不下去。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Why don't you retire?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山遂珍重掲簾而出。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">見外面黒却回云、外面黒。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tokusan made his bows and
lifted the blinds to withdraw, but he was met by darkness. Turning back
to Ryûtan, he said, "It is dark outside."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">潭乃點紙燭度與。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Ryûtan lit a paper candle and
handed it to him.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山擬接。潭便吹滅。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tokusan was about to take it
when Ryûtan blew it out.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山於此忽然有省。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">便作禮。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">At this, all of a sudden,
Tokusan went through a deep experience and made bows.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">潭云、子見箇甚麼道理。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Ryûtan said, "What sort of
realization do you have?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山云、某甲從今日去不疑天下老和尚舌頭也。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"From now on," said Tokusan, "I
will not doubt the words of an old oshõ who is renowned everywhere under
the sun."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">至明日、龍潭陞堂云、可中有箇漢、牙如劍樹、口似血盆。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The next day Ryûtan ascended
the rostrum and said, "I see a fellow among you. His fangs are like the
sword tree. His mouth is like a blood bowl.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">一棒打不回頭。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Strike him with a stick, and he
won't turn his head to look at you.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">他時異日、向孤峰頂上立君道在。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Someday or other, he will climb
the highest of the peaks and establish our Way there."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山遂取疏抄於法堂前、將一炬火提起云、窮諸玄辨、若一毫致於太虚、竭世樞機似一滴投於巨壑。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tokusan brought his notes on
the *Diamond Sutra*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> to the
front of the hall, pointed to them with a torch, and said, "Even though
you have exhausted the abtruse doctrines, it is like placing a hair in a
vast space. Even though you have learned all the secrets of the world,
it is like a drop of water dripped on the great ocean."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">將疏抄便燒。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">And he burned all his
notes.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">於是禮辭。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Then, making bows, he took his
leave of his teacher.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、徳山未出關時、心憤憤、口</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">□□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black">、得得來南方要滅却教外別傳之旨。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Before Tokusan crossed the
barrier from his native place, his mind burned and his mouth uttered
bitterness. He went soutward, intending to stamp out the doctrines of
special transmission outside the sutras.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">及到</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">澧</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">州路上問婆子買點心。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When he reached the road to
Reishû, he asked an old woman to let him have lunch to "refresh the
mind."<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">婆云、大徳車子内是甚麼文字。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Your worship, what sort of
literature do you carry in your pack?" the old woman asked.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">山云、金剛經疏抄。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Commentaries on the *Diamond
Sutra*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">,"
replied Tokusan.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">婆云、只如經中道、過去心不可得、見在心不可得、未來心不可得。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The old woman said, "I hear it
is said in that sutra, 'The past mind cannot be held, the present mind
cannot be held, the future mind cannot be held.'</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">大徳、要點那箇心。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Now, I would like to ask you,
what mind are you going to have refreshed?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">徳山被者一問、直得口似</span><span
lang="JA"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:
JA">□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;
color:black">檐。</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">At this question Tokusan was
dumbfounded.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">然雖如是、未肯向婆子句下死却。遂問婆子、近處有甚麼宗師。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">However, he did not remain
inert under her words but asked, "Do you know of any good teacher around
here?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">婆云、五里外有龍潭和尚。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The old woman said, "Five miles
from here you will find Ryûtan Oshõ."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">及到龍潭納盡敗闕。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Coming to Ryûtan, Tokusan got
the worst of it.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">可謂是前言不應後語。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">His former words were
inconsistent with his later ones.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">龍潭大似憐兒不覺醜。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">As for Ryûtan, he seemed to
have lost all sense of shame in his compassion toward his son.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">見他有些子火種、郎忙將惡水驀頭一澆澆殺。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Finding a bit of live coal in
the other, enough to start a fire, he hurriedly poured on muddy water to
annihilate everything at once.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">冷地看來、一場好笑。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A little cool reflection tells
us it was all a farce.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">聞名不如見面</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Hearing
the name cannot surpass seeing the face;<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">見面不如聞名</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Seeing
the face cannot surpass hearing the name.<span
style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">雖然救得鼻孔</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">He may
have saved his nose,<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">爭奈瞎却眼晴</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">But
alas! he lost his eyes.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
29**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> The
Sixth Patriarch's "Your Mind Moves"<span style="mso-tab-count:1">  
</span><span style="mso-tab-count:1">              </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">二十九　非風非幡</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">六祖、因風</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">颺</span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">刹幡。有二僧、對論。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The wind was flapping a temple
flag, and two monks started an argument.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">一云、幡動。一云、風動。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">One said the flag moved, the
other said the wind moved;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">往復曾未契理。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">they argued back and forth but
could not reach a conclusion.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">祖云、不是風動、不是幡動、仁者心動。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The Sixth Patriarch said, "It
is not the wind that moves, it is not the flag that moves; it is your
mind that moves."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">二僧悚然。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The two monks were
awe-struck.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、不是風動、不是幡動、不是心動、甚處見祖師。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">It is not the wind that moves;
it is not the flag that moves; it is not the mind that moves. How do you
see the patriarch?<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若向者裏見得親切、方知二僧買鐵得金。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you come to understand this
matter deeply, you will see that the two monks got gold when buying
iron.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">祖師忍俊不禁、一場漏逗。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The patriarch could not
withhold his compassion and courted disgrace.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">風幡心動</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Wind,
flag, mind, moving,<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">一状領過</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">All
equally to blame.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">只知開口</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Only
knowing how to open his mouth,<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">不覺話墮</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Unaware
of his fault in talking.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
30**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Baso's
"This Very Mind Is the Buddha"<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">三十　即心即佛</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">馬祖、因大梅問、如何是佛。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Daibai asked Baso, "What is the
Buddha?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">祖云、即心是佛。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Baso answered, "This very mind
is the Buddha."<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">無門曰、若能直下領略得去、著佛衣、喫佛飯、説佛話、行佛行、即是佛也。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you directly grasp Baso's
meaning, you wear the Buddha's clothes, eat the Buddha's food, speak the
Buddha's words, do the Buddha's deeds—that is, you are a Buddha
himself.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">然雖如是、大梅引多少人、錯認定盤星。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">However, alas! Daibai misled
not a few people into taking the mark on the balance for the weight
itself.<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">爭知道説箇佛字、三日漱口。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">How could he realize that even
mentioning the word "Buddha" should make us rinse out our mouths for
three days?<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">若是箇漢、見説即心是佛、掩耳便走。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If a man of understanding hears
anyone say, "This very mind is the Buddha," he will cover his ears and
rush away.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">青天白日</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The
blue sky and bright day,<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">切忌尋覓</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">No more
searching around!<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">更問如何</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"What
is the Buddha?" you ask:<span style="color:black"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;color:black">抱贓叫屈</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">With
loot in your pocket, you declare yourself innocent.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
31**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Jõshû
Investigates an Old Woman<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                   </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">三十一　趙州勘婆</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">趙州、因僧問婆子、臺山路向甚處去。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A monk asked an old woman,
"What is the way to Taisan?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">婆云、驀直去。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The old woman said, "Go
straight on."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">僧纔行三五歩。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">婆云、好箇師僧、又恁麼去。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When the monk had proceeded a
few steps, she said, "A good, respectable monk, but he too goes that
way."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">後有僧擧似州。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Afterward someone told Jõshû
about this.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">州云、待我去與</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">你</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">勘過這婆子。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Jõshû said, "Wait a bit, I will
go and investigate the old woman for you."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">明日便去亦如是問。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">婆亦如是答。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The next day he went and asked
the same question, and the old woman gave the same answer.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">州歸謂衆曰、臺山婆子、我與<span
lang="JA" style="mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span>勘破了也。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">On returning, Jõshû said to his
disciples, "I have investigated the old woman of Taisan for you."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、婆子只解坐籌帷幄、要且著賊不知。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The old woman only knew how to
sit still in her tent and plan the campaign; she did not know when she
was shadowed by a spy.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">趙州老人、善用偸營劫塞乃機、又且無大人相。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Though old Jõshû showed himself
clever enough to take a camp and overwhelm a fortress, he displayed no
trace of being a great commander.</span>

<span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-TW">撿</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">點將來、二倶有過。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If we look at them, they both
have their faults.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">且道、那裏是趙州、勘破婆子處。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">But tell me, what did Jõshû see
in the old woman?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">問既一般</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>The question was like the others,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">答亦相似</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>The answer was the same.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">飯裏有砂</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Sand in the rice,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">泥中有刺</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Thorns in the mud.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
32**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> A
Non-Buddhist Philosopher Questions the Buddha<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">              </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">三十二　外道問佛</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">世尊、因外道問、不問有言、不問無言。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A non-Buddhist philosopher said
to the Buddha, "I do not ask for words; I don not ask for
non-words."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">世尊據座。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The Buddha just sat
there.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">外道贊歎云、世尊大慈大悲、開我迷雲令我得入。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The philosopher said
admiringly, "The World-honored One, with his great mercy, has blown away
the clouds of my illusion and enabled me to enter the Way."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">乃具禮而去。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">And after making bows, he took
his leave.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">阿難尋問佛、外道有何所證贊歎而去。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Then Ananda asked the Buddha,
"What did he realize, to admire you so much?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">世尊云、如世良馬見鞭影而行。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The World-honored One replied,
"A fine horse runs even at the shadow of the whip."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、阿難乃佛弟子、宛不如外道見解、且道、外道與佛弟子相去多少。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Ananda was the Buddha's
disciple, but his understanding was not equal to that of the
non-Buddhist. I want to ask you, what difference is there between the
Buddha's disciple and the non-Buddhist?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">劍刃上行</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>On the edge of a sword,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">氷綾上走</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Over the ridge of an iceberg,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">不渉階梯</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>With no steps, no ladders,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">懸崖撒手</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Climbing the cliffs without hands.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
33**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Baso's
"No Mind, No Buddha"<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                         </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">三十三　非心非佛</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">馬祖、因僧問、如何是佛。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A monk asked Baso, "What is the
Buddha?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">祖曰、非心非佛。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Baso answered, "No mind, no
Buddha."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、若向者裏見得、參學事畢。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you understand this, you
have finished studying Zen.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">路逢劍客須呈</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>Present a sword if you meet a swordsman;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">不遇詩人莫獻</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>Don't offer a poem unless you meet a poet.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">逢人且説三分</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>When talking, tell one-third of it;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">未可全施一片</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>Don't divulge the whole at once.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
34**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Nansen's "Reason Is Not the Way"<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                  </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">三十四　智不是道</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">南泉云、心不是佛、智不是道。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Nansen said, "Mind is not the
Buddha, reason is not the Way."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、南泉可謂、老不識羞。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Nansen, growing old, had no
shame.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">纔開臭口、家醜外揚。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Just opening his stinking
mouth, he let slip the family secrets.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">然雖如是、知恩者少。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Yet there are very few who are
grateful for his kindness.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">天晴日頭出</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1"> </span>The sky clears, the sun shines bright,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">雨下地上濕</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1"> </span>The rain comes, the earth gets wet.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">盡情都説了</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1"> </span>He opens his heart and expounds the whole secret,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">只恐信不及</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1"> </span>But I fear he is little appreciated.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
35**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Seijõ's Soul Separated<span style="mso-tab-count:2">               
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">三十五　倩女離魂</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">五祖問僧云、倩女離魂、那箇是眞底。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Goso said to his monks,
"Seijõ's soul separated from her being. Which was the real
Seijõ?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、若向者裏悟得眞底、便知出殻入殻如宿旅舎。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When you realize what the real
is, you will see that we pass from one husk to another like travelers
stopping for a night's lodging.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">其或未然、切莫亂走。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">But if you do not realize it
yet, I earnestly advise you not to rush about wildly.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">驀然地水火風一散、如落湯</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">螃</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">蟹七手八脚。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When earth, water, fire, and
air suddenly separate, you will be like a crab struggling in boiling
water with its seven or eight arms and legs.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">那時莫言、不道。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When that happens, don't say I
didn't warn you!</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">雲月是同</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>The moon above the clouds is ever the same;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">渓山各異</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Valleys and mountains are separate from each
other.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">萬福萬福</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>All are blessed, all are blessed;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">是一是二</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Are they one or are they two?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
36**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> When
You Meet a Man of the Way<span style="mso-tab-count:2">                
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">三十六　路逢達道</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">五祖曰、路逢達道人、不將語默對、且道、將甚麼對。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Goso said, "When you meet a man
of the Way on the path, do not meet him with words or in silence. Tell
me, how will you meet him?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、若向者裏對得親切、不妨慶快。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">In such a case, if you can
manage an intimate meeting with him it will certainly be
gratifying.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">其或未然、也須一切處著眼。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">But if you cannot, you must be
watchful in every way.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">路逢達道人</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
2">              </span>Meeting a man of the Way on the road,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">不將語默對</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
2">              </span>Meet him with neither words nor silence.</span>

<span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-TW">攔</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">腮劈面拳</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>A punch on the jaw:</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">直下會便會</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
2">              </span>Understand, if you can directly
understand.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
37**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Jõshû's Oak Tree<span style="mso-tab-count:2">                          
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">三十七　庭前栢樹</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">趙州、因僧問、如何是祖師西來意。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A monk asked Jõshû, "What is
the meaning of Bodhidharma's coming to China?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">州云、庭前栢樹子。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Jõshû said, "The oak tree in
the garden."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、若向趙州答處見得親切、前無釋迦後無彌勒。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you understand Jõshû's
answer intimately, there is no Shakya before you, no Maitreya to
come.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">言無展事</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Words cannot express things;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">語不投機</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Speech does not convey the spirit.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">承言者喪</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Swayed by words, one is lost;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">滯句者迷</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Blocked by phrases, one is belwildered.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
38**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> A
Buffalo Passes the Window<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                           </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">三十八　牛過窓櫺</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">五祖曰、譬如水</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">牯</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">牛過窓櫺、頭角四蹄都過了、因甚麼尾巴過不得。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Goso said, "A buffalo passes by
the window. His head, horns, and four legs all go past. But why can't
the tail pass too?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、若　向者裏顛倒、著得一隻眼、下得一轉語、可以上報四恩下資三有。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you make a complete
about-face, open your eye, and give a turning word on this point, you
will be able to repay the four kinds of love that have favored you and
help the sentient beings in the three realms who follow you.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">其或未然、更須照顧尾巴始得。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you are still unable to do
this, return to this tail and reflect upon it, and then for the first
time you will realize something.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">過去墮抗</span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">塹</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">         </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Passing
by, it falls into a ditch;<span
style="mso-fareast-language:JA"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">回來却被壞</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
2">              </span>Coming back, all the worse, it is lost.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">者些尾巴子</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
2">              </span>This tiny little tail,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">直是甚奇怪</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
2">              </span>What a strange thing it is!</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
39**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> A
Mistake in Speaking<span style="mso-tab-count:2">               
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">三十九　雲門話墮</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">雲門、因僧問、光明寂照遍河沙。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A monk said to Unmon, "The
brilliance of the Buddha silently illuminates the whole universe. .
."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">一句未絶、門遽曰、豈不是張拙秀才語。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">But before the could finish the
verse, Unmon said, "Aren't those the words of Chõetsu the
Genius?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">僧云、是。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Yes, they are," answered the
monk.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">門云、話墮也。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"You have slipped up in your
speaking," Unmon said.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">後來、死心拈云、且道、那裏是者僧話墮處。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Afterward, Shishin Zenji
brought up the matter and said, "Tell me, at what point did the monk err
in his speaking?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、若向者裏見得雲門用處孤危、者僧因甚話墮、堪與人天爲師。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you clearly understand this
and realize how exacting Unmon was in his method, and what made the monk
err in his speaking, you are qualified to be a teacher of heaven and
earth.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">若也未明、自救不了。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you are not yet clear about
it, you are far from saving yourself.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">急流垂釣</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>A line cast in the rapids,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">貪餌者著</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>The greedy will be caught.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">口縫纔開</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Before you start to open your mouth,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">性命喪却</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Your life is already lost!</span>
