<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
40**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Tipping Over a Water Bottle<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                 </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">四十　<span
lang="JA" style="mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span>倒淨瓶</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-TW">溈</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">山和尚、始在百丈會中充典座。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When Isan Oshõ was with
Hyakujõ, he was *tenzo*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
\[</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">典座</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> head
cook\] of the monastery.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">百丈、將選大</span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">溈</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">主人。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">乃請同　首座對衆下語、出格者可往。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Hyakujõ wanted to choose a
master for Mount Tai-i, so he called together all the monks and told
them that anyone who could answer his question in an outstanding manner
would be chosen.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">百丈遂拈淨瓶、置地上設問云、不得喚作淨瓶、汝喚作甚麼。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Then he took a water bottle and
stood it on the floor, and said, "You may not call this a water bottle.
What do you call it?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">首座乃云、不可喚作木<span lang="JA"
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span>也。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The head monk said, "It cannot
be called a stump."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">百丈却問於山。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Hyakujõ asked Isan his
opinion.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">山乃<span lang="JA"
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span>倒淨瓶而去。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Isan tipped over the water
bottle with his feet and went out.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">百丈笑云、第一座　輸却山子也。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Hyakujõ laughed and said, "The
head monk loses."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">因命之爲山。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">And Isan was named as the
founder of the new monastery.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、</span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">溈</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">山一期之勇、爭奈跳百丈圈</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">圚</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">不出、</span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">撿</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">點將來、便重不便輕。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Isan displayed great spirit in
his action, but he could not cut himself free from Hyakujõ's apron
strings. He preferred the heavier task to lighter one.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">何故。<span lang="JA"
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span>。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Why was he like that,
eh?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">脱得盤頭、擔起鐵枷。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">He took off his headband to
bear the iron yoke.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;color:black;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">颺</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">下笊籬并木杓</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>Tossing bamboo baskets and ladles away,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">當陽一突絶周遮</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">    </span>He made a glorious dash and swept all before him.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">百丈重關欄不住</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">    </span>Hyakujõ's barrier cannot stop his advance;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">脚尖<span lang="JA"
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span>出佛如麻</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">    </span>Thousands of Buddhas come forth from the tips of his
feet.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
41**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Bodhidharma's Mind-Pacifying<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                         </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">四十一　達磨安心</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">達磨面壁。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Bodhidharma sat facing the
wall.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">二祖立雪。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The Second Patriarch stood in
the snow.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">斷臂云、弟子心未安、乞師安心。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">He cut off his arm and
presented it to Bodhidharma, crying, "My mind has no peace as yet! I beg
you, master, please pacify my mind!"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">磨云、將心來爲汝安。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Bring your mind here and I
will pacify it for you," replied Bodhidharma.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">祖云、覓心了不可得。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"I have searched for my mind,
and I cannot take hold of it," said the Second Patriarch.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">磨云、爲汝安心竟。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">"Now your mind is pacified,"
said Bodhidharma.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、<span lang="JA"
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span>齒老胡、十万里航海特特而來。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The broken-toothed old Hindu
came so importantly, thousands of miles over the sea.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">可謂是無風起浪。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">This was raising waves where
there was no wind.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">末後接得一箇門人、又却六根不具。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">In his last years he induced
enlightenment in his disciple, who, to make matters worse, was defective
in the six roots.</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">。謝三郎不識四字。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Why, Shasanro did not know for
ideographs.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">西來直指</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Coming east, directly pointing,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">事因囑起</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>You entrusted the Dharma, and trouble arose;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">撓聒叢林</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>The clamor of the monasteries</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">元來是<span lang="JA"
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span></span><span style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">      </span>Is all because of you.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
42**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> The
Girl Comes out of Samadhi<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                       </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">四十二　女子出定</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">世尊、昔、因文殊、至諸佛集處値諸佛各還本處。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Once, in the old days, in the
time of the World-honored One, Manjusri went to the assembly of the
Buddhas and found that everyone had departed to his original dwelling
place.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">惟有一女人近彼佛坐入於三昧。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Only a girl remained, sitting
in samadhi close to the Buddha's throne.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">文殊乃白佛、云何女人得近佛坐而我不得。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Manjusri asked Shakyamuni
Buddha, "Why can the girl get near the Buddha's throne, while I
cannot?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">佛告文殊、汝但覺此女、令從三昧起、汝自問之。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Shakyamuni Buddha said, "Bring
her out of her samadhi and ask her yourself."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">文殊遶女人三<span lang="JA"
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span>、鳴指一下、乃托至梵天盡其神力而不能出。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Manjusri walked around the girl
three times, snapped his fingers once, took her to the Brahma heaven,
and exerted all his miraculous powers to bring her out of her
meditation, but in vain.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">世尊云、假使百千文殊亦出此女人定不得。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The World-honored One said,
"Even a hundred thousand Manjusris cannot make her wake up.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">下方過一十二億河沙國土有罔明菩薩。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">But down below, past twelve
hundred million lands as innumerable as the sands of Ganges, there is a
Bodhisattva Mõmyõ.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">能出此女人定。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">He will be able to rouse her
from her samadhi."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">須臾罔明大士、從地湧出禮拜世尊。世尊敕罔明。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Instantly the Bodhisattva Mõmyõ
emerged from the earth and made a bow to the World-honored One, who gave
him his imperial order.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">却至女人前鳴指一下。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The Bodhisattva went over to
the girl and snapped his fingers once.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">女人於是從定而出。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">At this she came out of her
samadhi.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、釋迦老子、做者一場雜劇、不通小小。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Old Shakyamuni put a petty
drama on the stage and failed to enlighten the masses.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">且道、文殊是七佛之師、因甚出　女人定不得。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">I want to ask you: Manjusri is
the teacher of the Seven Buddhas; why couldn't he arouse the girl from
her samadhi?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">罔明初地菩薩、爲甚却出得。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">How was it that Mõmyõ, a
Bodhisattva at the beginner's stage, could do it?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">若向者裏見得親切、業識忙忙那伽大定。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you understand this
intimately, you will enjoy Nagya's grand samadhi in the busiest activity
of consciousness.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">出得出不得</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1"> </span>One was successful, the other was not;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">渠儂得自由</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1"> </span>Both secured freedom of mind.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">神頭并鬼面</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1"> </span>One in a god-mask, the other in a devil-mask;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">敗闕當風流</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1"> </span>Even in defeat, a beautiful performance.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
43**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Shuzan's Shippei<span style="mso-tab-count:2">             
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">四十三　首山竹篦</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">首山和尚、拈竹篦示衆云、汝等諸人、若喚作竹篦則觸。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Shuzan Oshõ held up his
*shippei*</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
\[staff of office\] before his disciples and said, "You monks! If you
call this a shippei, you oppose its reality.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">不喚作竹篦則背。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you do not call it a
shippei, you ignore the fact.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">汝諸人、且道、喚作甚麼。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tell me, you monks, what will
you call it?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、喚作竹篦則觸。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you call it a shippei, you
oppose its reality.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">不喚作竹篦則背。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you do not call it a
shippei, you ignore the fact.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">不得有語、不得無語。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Words are not available;
silence is not available.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">速道、速道。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Now, tell me quickly, what is
it?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">拈起竹篦</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Holding up the shippei,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">行殺活令</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>He takes life, he gives life.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">背觸交馳</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Opposing and ignoring interweave.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">佛祖乞命</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Even Buddhas and patriarchs beg for their lives.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
44**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Bashõ's Staff<span style="mso-tab-count:2">                    
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">四十四　芭蕉</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">拄</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">杖</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">芭蕉和尚示衆云、</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">你</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">有</span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-TW">拄</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">杖子、我興</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">你</span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">
</span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">拄</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">杖子。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Bashõ Osho said to his
disciples, "If you have a staff, I will give you a staff.</span>

<span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-TW">你</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">拄</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">杖子、我奪</span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">你</span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">
</span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">拄</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">杖子。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you have no staff, I will
take it from you."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、扶過斷橋水、伴歸無月村。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">It helps me wade across a river
when the bridge is down. It accompanies me to the village on a moonless
night.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">若喚作</span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">拄</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">杖、入地獄如箭。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
JA"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you call it a staff, you
will enter hell like an arrow.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">諸方深與淺</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1"> </span><span style="mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">              </span></span>The depths and shallows of the world<span
style="mso-fareast-language:JA"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">都在掌握中</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1"> </span><span style="mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">              </span></span>Are all in its grasp.<span
style="mso-fareast-language:JA"></span></span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">天<span
lang="JA" style="mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span></span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-TW">拄</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">地</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">         </span>It supports the heaven and sustains the earth.<span
style="mso-fareast-language:JA"></span></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">隨處振宗風</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1"> </span><span style="mso-fareast-language:JA"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">              </span></span>Everywhere, it enhances the
doctrine.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
45**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> Hõen's
"Who Is He?"<span style="mso-tab-count:2">                 
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">四十五　他是阿誰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">東山演師祖曰、釋迦彌勒猶是他奴。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Hõen of Tõzan said, "Even
Shakya and Maitreya are servants of another.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">且道、他是阿誰。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">I want to ask you, who is
he?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、若也見得他分曉、譬如十字街頭撞見親爺相似、更不須問別人道是與不是。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you can really see this
"another" with perfect clarity, it is like encountering your own father
at a crossroads. Why should you ask whether you recognize him or
not?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">他弓莫挽</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Don't draw another's bow,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">他馬莫騎</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Don't ride another's horse,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">他非莫辨</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Don't discuss another's faults,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">他事莫知</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">      </span>Don't explore another's affairs.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
46**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Proceed On from the Top of the Pole<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">            </span><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">              </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">四十六　竿頭進歩</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">石霜和尚云、百尺竿頭、如何進歩。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Sekisõ Oshõ asked, "How can you
proceed on further from the top of a hundred-foot pole?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">又古徳云、百尺竿頭坐底人、雖然得入未爲眞。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Another eminent teacher of old
said, "You, who sit on the top of a hundred-foot pole, although you have
entered the Way you are not yet genuine.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">百尺竿頭、須進歩十方世界現全身。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Proceed on from the top of the
pole, and you will show your whole body in the ten directions."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、進得歩、翻得身、更嫌何處不稱尊。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you go on further and turn
your body about, no place is left where you are not the master.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">然雖如是、且道、百尺竿頭、如何進歩。</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">嗄</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">But even so, tell me, how will
you go on further from the top of a hundred-foot pole? Eh?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">瞎却頂門眼</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1"> </span>He darkens the third eye of insight</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">錯認定盤星</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1"> </span>And clings to the first mark on the scale.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">拌身能捨命</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1"> </span>Even though he may sacrifice his life,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">一盲引衆盲</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1"> </span>He is only a blind man leading the blind.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
47**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Tosotsu's Three Barriers<span
style="mso-tab-count:2">                         </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">四十七　兜率三關</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">兜率悦和尚、設三關問學者、</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tosotsu Etsu Oshõ set up three
barriers for his disciples:</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">撥草參玄只圖見性。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**1.**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> You leave no stone unturned to
explore profundity, simply to see into your true nature.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">即今上人性在甚處。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Now, I want to ask you, just at
this moment, where is your true nature?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">識得自性方脱生死。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**2.**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> If you realize your true
nature, you are free from life and death.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">眼光落時、作麼生脱。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Tell me, when your eyesight
deserts you at the last moment, how can you be free from life and
death?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">脱得生死便知去處、四大分離向甚處去。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**3.**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> When you set yourself free
from life and death, you should know your ultimate destination. So when
the four elements separate, where will you go?</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、若能下得此三轉語、便可以隨處作主遇縁即宗。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you can put turning words to
these three questions, you are the master wherever you may stand and
command Zen whatever circumstances you may be in.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">其或未然、麁<span lang="JA"
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span>易飽、細嚼難飢。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If otherwise, listen: gulping
down your meal will fill you easily, but chewing it well can sustain
you.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">一念普觀無量劫</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">    </span>This moment's thoughts sees through eternal time;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無量劫事即如今</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">    </span>Eternal time is just this moment.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">如今<span lang="JA"
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span>破箇一念</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">    </span>If you see through this moment's thought,</span>

<span lang="JA" style="font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45;mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">破如今<span
lang="JA" style="mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span>底人</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">    </span>You see through the man who sees through this
moment.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Case
48**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
Kempõ's One Road<span style="mso-tab-count:2">                     
</span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">四十八　乾峰一路</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">乾峰和尚、因僧問、十方薄伽梵、一路涅槃門。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">A monk asked Kempõ Oshõ, "It is
written, 'Bhagavats in the ten directions. One straight road to
Nirvana.'</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">未審路頭在甚麼處。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">I still wonder where the road
can be."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">峰拈起</span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">拄</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">杖、劃一劃云、在者裏。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Kempõ lifted his staff, drew a
line, and said, "Here it is."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">後僧請益雲門。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Later the monks asked the same
question to Unmon,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">門拈起扇子云、扇子<span lang="JA"
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span>跳上三　十三天、築著帝釋鼻孔。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">who held up his fan and said,
"This fan jumps up to the thirty-third heaven and hits the nose of the
deity Sakra Devanam Indra.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">東海鯉魚、打一棒雨似盆傾。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When you strike the carp of the
eastern sea, the rain comes down in torrents."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Comment**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門曰、一人向深深海底行、<span
lang="JA"
style="mso-fareast-language:JA">□</span>土揚塵、一人於高高山頂、白浪滔天。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">One, going to the bottom of the
sea, lifts up clouds of dust; the other, on the top of the highest
mountain, rises towering waves to wash the sky.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">把定放行、各出一隻手扶竪宗乗。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">One holding fast, the other
letting go, each stretches out his hand to support the profound
teaching.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">大似兩箇馳子相撞著。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">They are just like two riders
starting from opposite ends of the course and meeting in the
middle.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">世上應無直底人。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">But none on earth can be
absolutely direct.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">正眼觀來二大老惣未識路頭在。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When examined with a true eye,
neither of these two great masters knows the road.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's Verse**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">頌曰</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">未擧歩時先已到</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">    </span>Before a step is taken, the goal is reached;</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">未動舌時先説了</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">    </span>Before the tongue is moved, the speech is finished.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">直饒著著在機先</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">    </span>Though each move is ahead of the next,</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">更須知有向上竅</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">    </span>There is still a transcendent secret.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Mumon's
Postscript**</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
2">                       </span></span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">後序</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">從上佛祖垂示機縁、據款結案、初無剰語。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">The sayings and doings of the
Buddha and the patriarchs have been set down in their original
form.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">掲翻腦蓋、露出眼睛。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Nothing superfluous has been
added by the author, who has taken the lid off his head and exposed his
eyeballs.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">肯要諸人直下承當、不從佗覓。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Your direct realization is
demanded; it should not be sought through others.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">若是通方上士。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">纔聞擧著、便知落處。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you are a man of
realization, you will immediately grasp the point at the slightest
mention of it.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">了無門戸可入、亦無階級可升。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">There is no gate for you to go
through; there are no stairs for you to ascend.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">掉臂度關不問關吏。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">You pass the checkpoint,
squaring your shoulders, without asking permission of the keeper.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">豈不見玄沙道、無門解脱之門、無意道人之意。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Remember Gensha's saying,
"No-gate is the gate of emancipation; no-meaning is the meaning of the
man of the Way."</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">又白雲道、明明知道只是者箇、爲甚麼透不過。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">And Hakuun says, "Clearly you
know how to talk of it, but why can't you pass this simple, specific
thing?"</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">恁麼説話、也是赤土</span><span
lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW">搽</span><span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">牛</span><span lang="ZH-TW"
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Apple LiGothic Medium&quot;;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-TW">嬭</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">However, all this kind of talk
is like making a mud pie with milk and butter.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">若透得無門關、早是鈍置無門。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If you have passed the
Mumonkan, you can make a fool of Mumon.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">若透不得無門關、亦之辜負自己。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">If not, you are betraying
yourself.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">所謂、涅槃心易曉、差別智難明。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">It is easy to know the Nirvana
mind but difficult to attain the wisdom of differentiation.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">明得差別智、家國自安寧。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">When you have realized this
wisdom, peace and order will reign over your land.</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">時紹定改元　解制前五日</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">*The change of era to Jõtei
\[1228\], five days before the end of summer session*</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">楊岐八世孫　無門比丘慧開　謹識。</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">*Respectfully inscribed by
Mumon Ekai Bhikkhu, eighth in succession from Yõgi*</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Osaka\2212\7B49\5E45">無門關　巻終</span><span
style="font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">Wu-wen kuan (Mumonkan)<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">          </span>End of the book</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">**Source**</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">English
translation by late Zen master *Katsuki Sekida*</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> (*Two Zen
Classics*</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">
26-137)</span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>

<span style="font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span>
